<time>1489793129174< /time><Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
The place was very clean in appearance. The food was a little above average with good presentation. The chips and salsa were a bit of a disappointment because I was chips and pico like you get at most places; however, the 'salsa' is the same hot sauce they give you with your food... plus it was only a very small amount of chips. Main dish was tasty and came out very quickly (I was the only one in the restaurant). Very small menu... like, there isn't even tacos on the menu... kind of disappointed with the small menu and lack of options. Overall, the main dish was very good!< /Review>

<Text>Simple looking place. Simple layout, looks like it is a fast food place! Order at the counter and then they bring it to your table. Nice. The menu is painted on the wall, and I suggest you love lamb if you come here. It is the specialty of the house. It is oh so tender and tasty. The salsa comes in two flavors and warm and hotter. I liked them both and found the warm  to be excellent and the hot was a bit hotter than I wanted. The hand made tortillas were excellent and were gobbled up promptly.
The dessert flan was excellent and greatly appreciated! All in all my cousin who is a local, now tells me that this a new favorite of hers! Were were all pleased and stuffed! Coming back soon, I hope!
oh yes, be patient, food is prepared in small batches and is oh so fresh and wonderful.< /Text><Rating>5</Rating>< Name>

2 orders of Tortillas (3 tortillas/order)
Then a side of each of these:
Beans
Rice
Guac
Soyrizo

Extremely disappointed in Hawke Media! Prior to hiring them, I had successfully ran ads but had little time to manage them. Thought I'd hire a "professional" team to offload the work... Oh, how I was wrong...

They ran the ads for two months, me pointing out multiple of their rookie (account manager assigned) mistakes throughout the process.

I understand that results are not guaranteed and am completely fine with that but the overwhelming horrendous work they've done is completely unacceptable.

Absolutely no activity from the few ads they've launched and tweaked for over two months. Seemed like a bunch of amateurs work there. They did not deliver on the agreement that they put in place. Have not met deadlines they set. Furthermore, the multiple phases of work to be completed they put in place have not been completed in a timely manner and some not completed at all.

I paused the payment and asked them to complete the agreed upon work before I pay them again. Their amateur response was "we will not do any work until payment is made" REALLY? I paid you for work, please complete it!

I have then tried to connect with them by phone, email and postal mail, have made 15+ attempts. There has been absolutely no response to my emails. No call backs for the voice messages I left. When I was able to connect with their tech support department & explained the situation, the promised call backs never took place.

At this point I gave up... Not worth my time... I would highly discourage anyone looking into hiring Hawke Media.

< text>
~No approvals for app installation. Yes, they installed a web app without our approval! We noticed when our sales dropped significantly and when we researched the issue we figured out the problem. Apps slow down websites and impact the customer experience.

~Adwords: We purchased the lower level management fee option of $2k per month based on a monthly ad spend of $1-$10k. This was great because our current ad spend was just under $1k, and we fell within this service level for managing our existing account.

Here are their rates with no fine print on spending.
$1-$10,000, 2k management fee
$10,001-$25,000 20% of monthly add spend
$25,001-$50,000 15% of monthly add spend
$50,001+             10% of monthly add spend

So you can imagine our surprise when the media team, without consulting us, upped our adword spend and we received a $4k+ CC bill. When we asked what happened ~ they said they had carte blanche to spend up to $1-$10k when we signed up for the 2k management fee. Would you have assumed based on the rates above that they could spend whatever they wanted? What about on the $50,001+ no end in sight monthly ad spend? To me, it read as a service level agreement where we choose the budget, & they'll manage the spend. We would have never approved a 4k spend. As a small business, this was crushing.

~Mailchimp campaign work was a mess (and that's putting it mildly).  From promotional codes not being programmed, follow-up newsletter campaigns not being scheduled, and reminder emails not being complete, we ended up spending more time managing this then just doing it ourselves, and the creative was just underwhelming.

~Their webwork needed webwork (lots of examples here, let's just say hard pass).

~Strategy. If you don't know your demographic or competitive landscape, then they'll figure this out and do a wonderful job presenting it. If you know all about your company + competitors, pass on strategy. They won't put out a sales plan to increase your numbers, just tell you all about your business - which is fine if you don't know yourself and want to get to know yourself.

~Billing. They are saying we have a 334.62$ bill outstanding for 3rd party services (that we were not using at the time). You'd think after their 4k unapproved media spend, unauthorized app download, mail chimp failures, they would just waive it, with a "we will try to do better next time". Instead they are sending us emails threatening us with legal action plus attorney's fees.

What we liked! Thus the additional star.

~Katie, the adwords developer was wonderful to work with. Be sure to manage your own budget, and come up with your own strategy.
~Graphics were great.
~James, the account guy, was groovy.</text>

<Rate>2<//Rate>< text>
It has been a long while since I have eaten at a Togo's.  Unfortunately it will be a long while before I go again.  Upon arrival there was another group sitting down eating their sandwiches.  There was no staff at the counter.  I waited a few minutes until I called out for an employee to assist me.  After three attempts, a seemingly preoccupied young lady came out from the backroom to take my order.  Being  unfamiliar with the menu and asking what my choices were as the sandwich was being made, the preoccupied server became almost surly in her attitude towards me.
For a large sandwich and a medium drink my total was $14. Overpriced in my opinion, the quality of the food was no better than a Subway sandwich.
As I only visit a Togo's eatery thrice a decade, I think I will stop altogether purely based on selection of ingredients, quality and price.  Any employee can have a bad day, but Togo's is not the experience I was looking for.<//text>

<Time>1505351991646</Time><Rate>5< /Rate><Review>Let me just start off by saying how I really do not enjoy going into a ANY kind of dealership. I had a 2015 Toyota Prius. I decided to bring it in because I wanted to see what kind of deal they had. I honestly went in there not even thinking I was going to buy another car. His approach was awesome. He was talking to me like a bro instead of those car people that linger over you.

I will have to say that Sean Cunningham ( our salesman ) who sold us this car and also the finance manager that helped us with our back and forth sales figures,  really were AWESOME. I admit I was quite standoffish mainly because I'm really not fan of this entire process.

After ALOT back-and-forth between whether I should get the Prius prime or the regular Prius,  I finally decided on getting the The Red 2017 Plug-In Prius Prime. I am so glad that I decided to pay a little extra to get the car that I really wanted. This car is absolutely insane ( in a good way) The plush leather interior, The 11.5 inch monster display. The fact that it has amazing gas mileage is a huge asset for me because I drive a lot. 25 miles on a single charge on EV mode (without touching the gasoline) once the PLUG IN battery is depleted, the gas/electric engine kicks in. 58 MPG I'm getting on Hybrid mode.

It has an AC button on the keyless key module that you press and hold it. It starts the AC up ( not the circulating fans) The AC before you get in the car?? Whaaaat?? How AWSOME!! And so needed since we live in the desert.

I purchased a used certified 2017 RAV 4 in Aug 2018. It looked and ran well. That summer a friend noticed that my back-up light did not light when I was backing-up. I went to the dealership and asked them to look into it. I started this in May 2018. Today, Feb. 5, 2020 the problem was resolved. Over a year and a half I have called repeatedly about getting the part and getting the light repaired. I spoke with Johnny Pipitt in person on 10/26/19, a weekend sharing my frustration with this issue as I had left repeated messages on Ricky Doremus' and Ivan Alvarodo's voice mails. My calls were not returned. I went in yesterday about this again, the part was ordered, installed and I was charged about half of what the charges were. The damage was from the previous owner,  I had no knowledge of it, but I could not prove it. So it was not covered in the certified agreement. Here is my point: Be careful and have any certified used vehicle you buy from this dealership inspected by a trusted outside mechanic.
This RAV 4 was the 3 vehicle I have purchased at this dealership. I will not be going back.< /text>

< review>
I haven't been to TOTD for many years. It was because my negative past experience and most of the comments I heard from others were very similar to my own. Poor customer service, untrustworthy representatives, unsatisfied work and so on. For years my impression of TOTD was this and for that reason I never returned or recommended TOTD, "until now.'

My "maintenance required" light came on. The two mechanics I was familiar with were no longer at the shops. I was pressed for time and couldn't think of any other place than TOTD. Reluctant, I found myself pulling into the service department. A courteous young man greeted me then directed me to a service representative. All I could think about was that I was setting myself up for complete disappointment. Not being one to hold back I shared this with Chase (Service Rep.). He could not be nicer. I felt absolutely no pressure to buy anything or even stay for that matter. He offered to have their complimentary shuttle take me to work. Ed The driver was like an OL Friend. We chatted the whole time.
When my car was finished Chase called me with several options. I went in with intentions of only having one thing done but, I left with having several things done. Not once did I feel like I was being pressured. Chase made me feel more like he truly cared and was suggesting options I might want to consider if I didn't want to have everything done at once.

My car feels great. Im very happy with the service provided by TOTD and especially from Chase & Ed. It's because of them I will be returning and looking forward to them caring for my car as if it were their own.

Thank you Toyota of the Desert & Thank you Chase & Ed!
